    <script type="text/javascript">
     function SetSectionNameAsClass() {
    var count = 0;
    document
      .querySelectorAll(".stream-post .widget:not(.proc-section)")
      .forEach(function (widget) {
        widget.classList.add("proc-section");
        //console.log("widget "+count++);
        if (widget.querySelector(".badge-name")) {
          //console.log("widget "+count+" has badge");
          if (
            widget.querySelector(".badge-name").innerText == "Z-17 Collective"
          ) {
            widget.classList.add("partner-container");
            //console.log("widget "+count+" has badge Z-17");
          }
          if (widget.querySelector(".badge-name").innerText == "PARTNERSHIPS") {
            widget.classList.add("partner-low-key-container");
            //console.log("widget "+count+" has badge PARTNERSHIPS");
          }
        }
      });
  }

  window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    if (document.getElementsByClassName("badge-name").length > 0) {
      if (
        document.getElementsByClassName("badge-name")[0].innerText ==
        "Z-17 Collective"
      ) {
        document
          .getElementsByClassName("post-partial")[0]
          .classList.add("partner-container");
        //console.log("it is the partner");
      }

      if (
        document.getElementsByClassName("badge-name")[0].innerText ==
        "PARTNERSHIPS"
      ) {
        document
          .getElementsByClassName("post-partial")[0]
          .classList.add("partner-low-key-container");
        //console.log("it is the low-key partner");
      }
    }

    SetSectionNameAsClass();
  });
    </script>

    <script>
     function createElementChangeListener(selector, callback) {
    const initializedNodes = new Set([]);

    document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach(node => {
        callback(node);
        initializedNodes.add(node);
    });

    const mutationObserver = new MutationObserver(() => {
        const nodes = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
        nodes.forEach(node => {
            if (!initializedNodes.has(node)) {
                callback(node);
                initializedNodes.add(node);
            }
        });
    });

    mutationObserver.observe(document.body, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true
    });
}
    </script>
    <!-- End User Code -->

window.REBELMOUSE_LOWEST_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        var navbarItems = document.querySelectorAll('.navbar-sections__item');

navbarItems.forEach(function(el) {
  var dropdown = el.querySelector('.navbar-sections__dropdown')
  if(dropdown) {
    el.onmouseover = function() {
      el.classList.add('active')
      if (typeof checkRunnerLazyLoadedItems === "function") {
        checkRunnerLazyLoadedItems();
      }
    }
    el.onmouseout = function() {
      el.classList.remove('active')
    }
    el.onclick = function() {
      el.classList.toggle('active')
    }
  }
});
    

});

window.REBELMOUSE_LOWEST_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        function VideoPlayerLoader() {
  let widgetsHead = document.querySelectorAll('div:not(.playlist-posts) .widget__head, div:not(.for-business) .widget__head');

  if(widgetsHead.length) {
    widgetsHead.forEach(function(widgetHead) {
      let video = widgetHead.querySelector('.widget__video');
      let image = widgetHead.querySelector('.widget__image');

      if (video) {
        const regex = /players\%2F([\w\-])+\.js/g;
        const script = video.querySelector('script[type="video-content"]');
        let str = '';

        if (script) {
          str = script.innerText;
        }
        //console.log('not null === ', str);
        if(str.length) {
          str = regex.exec(str);

          if (str !== null) {
            //console.log("STR != NULL", str);
            let videoPlayer = str[0].replace(/players\%2F/g, '').replace('.js', '').split('-');
            let videoWrapper = document.createElement('div');
            let videoPlayerScript = document.createElement('script');
            let is_sponsored_video = widgetHead.closest("article").querySelector(".badge-list-sponsored");

            if (location.pathname === '/') {
              videoPlayer[1] = 'qKoDmz4y';
            }
            if (location.pathname.indexOf('/videos/') == 0) {
              videoPlayer[1] = '72lJ7Q5V';
            }
            if (is_sponsored_video) {
              videoPlayer[1] = 'QdSUjqI8';
            }
            videoWrapper.id = 'botr_' + videoPlayer.join('_') + '_div';
            videoPlayerScript.src = 'https://content.jwplatform.com/players/' + videoPlayer.join('-') + '.js'
            videoPlayerScript.async = true;

            image.onclick = function () {
              //console.log('CLICK ON AN IMAGE', image);
              image.className += " hidden";
              video.style.display = "block";
              video.appendChild(videoWrapper);
              video.appendChild(videoPlayerScript);
            };
          } else { //copy from ui-basics to cover the rest of videos

            if (script) {
              image.onclick = function () {
                video.innerHTML = script.innerHTML;
                image.className += " hidden";
                video.style.display = "block";
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
  }
}

function clickSponsoredVideos() {
  var sponsored_videos = document.querySelectorAll(".badge-list-sponsored");
  for (var i = 0; i < sponsored_videos.length; i++) {
    var article = sponsored_videos[i].closest("article");
    if (
      article &&
      article.classList.contains("video-article") &&
      !article.classList.contains("image-clicked")
    ) {
      article.classList.toggle("image-clicked");
      article.querySelector(".widget__head .widget__image").click();
    }
  }
}

function clickPrimaryVideo() {
  var primary_video = document.querySelector(".container_main .video-article");
  if (primary_video && !primary_video.classList.contains('image-clicked')) {
    primary_video.classList.toggle("image-clicked");
    primary_video.querySelector(".widget__head .widget__image").click();
  }
}

createElementChangeListener("div:not(.playlist-posts) .widget__head, div:not(.for-business) .widget__head", (el) => {
  VideoPlayerLoader();
  if (location.pathname != '/videos/' && location.pathname.indexOf('/videos/') == 0) {
    clickPrimaryVideo();
  }
  clickSponsoredVideos();
});
    

});

window.REBELMOUSE_LOWEST_TASKS_QUEUE.push(function(){

    
        function full_height_all_the_things() {    
  var fullies = document.querySelectorAll(".fullheight:not(.fh_processed)");
  for (var i = 0; i < fullies.length; i++) {
    var this_fully = fullies[i];
    this_fully.classList.toggle("fh_processed");

    var fully_style = window.getComputedStyle(this_fully);
    if (fully_style.display == 'none') continue;

    try {
      var new_height = this_fully.closest(".row").offsetHeight + "px";
      this_fully.closest(".col").style.height = new_height;
      this_fully.style.height = new_height;
    } catch (e) {
      (console.error || console.log).call(console, e.stack || e);
    }
  }
}

function adjust_sticky_positioning() {    
  var wides = document.querySelectorAll(".sticky_wide");
  for (var i = 0; i < wides.length; i++) {
    if (wides[i].offsetParent === null) continue;

    try {
      var blk = wides[i].closest(".content_block_wrapper");
      var ldrbrd = wides[i].querySelector("div");
      var clmn = null;
      if (blk) clmn = blk.querySelector(".sticky_column");

      if (ldrbrd && ldrbrd.style.display !== 'none') {
        wides[i].style.display = 'block';
        if (clmn) clmn.style.top = "181px";
      } else {
        wides[i].style.display = 'none';
        if (clmn) clmn.style.top = "91px";
      }
    } catch (e) {
      (console.error || console.log).call(console, e.stack || e);
    }
  }
}       

document.addEventListener("scroll", function(event) {
  adjust_sticky_positioning();
  return this;
});

createElementChangeListener(".fullheight", (el) => {
  full_height_all_the_things();
});
    

});
